        <td id="LC374" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The licenses for most software are designed to take away your freedom to </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L375" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="375"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L376" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="376"></td>
        <td id="LC376" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">intended to guarantee your freedom to share and change free software--to </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L377" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="377"></td>
        <td id="LC377" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">make sure the software is free for all its users.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L378" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="378"></td>
        <td id="LC378" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L379" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="379"></td>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L381" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="381"></td>
        <td id="LC381" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Software Foundation and other authors who decide to use it. You can use </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L382" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="382"></td>
        <td id="LC382" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">it too, but we suggest you first think carefully about whether this </td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L386" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="386"></td>
        <td id="LC386" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When we speak of free software, we are referring to freedom of use, not </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>

</td>

      </tr>

</td>

</td>

</td>

</td>

        <td id="L431" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="431"></td>

      </tr>

</td>

</td>

</td>

</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L465" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="465"></td>
        <td id="LC465" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The precise terms and conditions for copying, distribution and </td>
      </tr>

</td>

        <td id="LC1339" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Creative Commons Corporation (&quot;Creative Commons&quot;) is not a law firm and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1340" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1340"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L1341" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1341"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1342" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1342"></td>

        <td id="L1343" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1343"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="LC1344" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">warranties regarding its licenses, any material licensed under their</td>

</td>

        <td id="L1351" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1351"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="LC1354" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and certain other rights specified in the public license below. The</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="L1358" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1358"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1359" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1359"></td>
        <td id="LC1359" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     intended for use by those authorized to give the public</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="LC1360" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     permission to use material in ways otherwise restricted by</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1361" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1361"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1362" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1362"></td>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1365" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1365"></td>
        <td id="LC1365" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     applying our licenses so that the public can reuse the</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

        <td id="LC1407" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  a. Adapted Material means material subject to Copyright and Similar</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1408" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1408"></td>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="LC1410" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     arranged, transformed, or otherwise modified in a manner requiring</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>

        <td id="LC1819" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">part a textbook of mathematics, a Secondary Section may not explain</td>
      </tr>
